< text>
High marks to the sales staff for the low pressure dealing and willingness to get us the car we wanted. Aaron jumped in a car and drove down to Gardenia and back from Ventura the afternoon we stopped in to get us the exact car we were after. Tony got us financing for under 3% and we had all docs signed and keys in our hand inside of an hour!

Lower marks to the quality of the car we purchased. After getting it home and giving it a good wash, I noted a poorly repaired rear bumper, a faulty headlight and several door dings. To their credit, Enterprise immediately took it back. They drove it to their maintenance facility in Sylmar. We got it back a week later (unwashed and with 1/8 tank of gas) with a professional repair/repainted bumper, but had to drop it off a few days later so that they could again drive it to Sylmar to replace the headlamp. After 3 weeks of ownership, Enterprise employees have put more mileage on my car than I have.  For paying top bluebook price for the car, I expected a near perfect car when driving it off the lot, not 3 weeks and 200mi later.

Would I buy from Enterprise again, yes. But I will be less forgiving next time.<//text>
